[cid:image002.jpg@01D01540.87B942A0]Dear Classmates,

I wish you all a joyous and peaceful holiday season.  It's a time when old =
friends like to reconnect-so why not share your latest news with classmates=
? Fill us in on the details of holiday gatherings with family and friends, =
life at work, your latest outdoor/travel adventure, or that really cool sno=
wman you sculpted the other day-anything that's happening in your life is w=
elcome in Scope class notes.

Just send a few lines to me at claire.a.solomon@gmail.com<mailto:claire.a.s=
olomon@gmail.com> by January 3rd- I'll be sure to get your news published i=
n the next (Spring '15) issue of Scope. (The Winter issue will be hitting y=
our mailbox in mid-January.)

Oh, and be sure to let me know if you plan to attend our 5th Reunion, May 2=
8-31, 2015! It's going to be great, so don't miss it! (For more information=
 on registration, housing, and activities, visit www.skidmore.edu/reunion<h=
ttp://www.skidmore.edu/reunion>).

All the best to you and yours,

Claire

Claire Solomon '10
